288a7(phal chen): par sprul pa de dag thams cad kyang mthong bar gyur to// shes par gyur to// nyams su myong bar gyur to// rnam par dpyad par gyur to// mtshan mar byas par gyur to// dmigs kyis/
288b1(phal chen): rtogs par gyur to// bdag nyid kyang de dag na 'dug par shes par gyur to// 'di lta ste/ dper na mi nang pa sems kyi rgyud tha ma byung bar gyur te// de ma thag tu skye ba'i sems nye bar gnas
288b2(phal chen): nas/ las kyi srid pa mngon du gyur na/ las ji lta bur byas shing bsags pa'i rnam par smin pas las mi dge ba'i rkyen gyis ni sems can dmyal ba dpa byol song gi skye gnas dang /
288b3(phal chen): yi dgas kyi yul lam/ gshin rje'i mi lag cha gnyems pa thogs pa gshe zhing khro ba dag kyang mthong bar gyur/ sems can dmyal ba pa'i dud mo dang // 'o dod kyi sgra'ang thos par
288b4(phal chen): gyur la/ ba tshwa'i chu de dag mthong ste spu gri'i sngo gshibs pa'i ri de dag dang / lcags kyi shal ma la'i sdong po de dag dang // ral gri'i so'i nags tshal de dag kyang mthong bar gyur pa
288b5(phal chen): sems can dmyal ba de dag kyang kun nas 'bar zhing yongs su 'bar ba dang / rab tu 'bar ba dang / lcags kyi bum pa gcig tu 'bar ba de dag kyang mthong bar gyur lag gnod pa de/
288b6(phal chen): ngag thams cad kyis kyang gnod par bya zhing // tshor ba de dag kyang nyams su myong ba tsam du shes par gyur te/ sems can dmyal ba pa de dag kyang me'i gdung bas sdug bsngal ba zhig tu
288b7(phal chen): mthong ngam/ bdag gis myong bar gyur tam// las dge ba'i tshogs kyis lha'i khang pa dang gnas shig mthong bar gyur tam/ lha'i 'khor dang / lha mo'i tshogs dang / rgyan rnam par
289a1(phal chen): phye ba thams cad kyang mthong bar gyur te/ bza' shing gi rab dang / dka' thub kyi nags tshal dang / chu klung dang / rdzing dang / rin po dang
289a2(phal chen): yid bzhin gyi shing dang / longs spyod mang po mthong ngam/ nyams su myong bar gyur te/ tshe'i yun kyang de dang mnyam par shes par gyur na// de ni 'di nas kyang 'phos pa med/
289a3(phal chen): der yang skyes pa med de/ mi snang bar ma gyur bzhin du/ las kyi yul bsam gyis mi khyab pas bya ba'i rnam pa de lta bu dag shes shing mthong la nyams su myong bar rung ngo // de bzhin /
289a4(phal chen): du tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs kyis byang chub sems dpa'i las kyi yul bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i phyir rgyar rnam par sprul pa de dag thams cad kyang mthong bar gyur to// 'di lta ste/
289a5(phal chen): dper na skyes bu 'byung po'i gdon gyis non pa ni// gzugs kyi rnam pa sna tshogs mang po mthong ste/ ci dris pa de dag gi lung yang ston to// de bzhin du tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs kyis/ byang
289a6(phal chen): chub semos dpa'i ye shes dang byin gyi rlabs kyi mthus rgyun de dag thams cad mthong bar gyur to// 'di lta ste/ dper na klu'i khang par phyin pa'i skyes bus ni klu'i 'du shes kyi rnam pa la
289a7(phal chen): nugs pas kyim gcigag ma nyi ma bdun ma/ zlab byeng ngam/ ma ba gcig gam/ lo gcig gam/ mi brgyar yang 'du shes kyi rnam pos shes te/ klu'i 'dushes kyi rnam pa dang thal nas/
289b1(phal chen): mi'i 'du shes kyi rnam par na lung tsam las ma lon par mthong ngo // de bzhin du tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs// byang chub sems dpa'i 'du shes kyi rnam pas ma btang ba'i tho dang ldar pas
289b2(phal chen): kyang / byang chub sems dpa' byams pa'i byin gyi rlabs kyis yud tsam gcig pu de'ang bskal pa bye ba khrag khrig brgya spong mang por shes par gyur to// 'di lta ste/ dper na tshangs pa chen po'i/
289b3(phal chen): gzhal med khang 'gro ba thams cad na rgyan gyi dam pa phul zhes bya ba yod de/ de'i nang du stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyang gzugs brnyan gyi tshul du dmigs pa
289b4(phal chen): thams cad dang ma 'dres par gsal bar snang ngo // de bzhin du tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs kyis kyang / rgyan de dag thams cad dmigs pa thams cad du phan tshun ma 'dres pa dang / phan tshun ma
289b5(phal chen): 'dzings par gzugs rab tu byung ba mthong ngo // 'di lta ste// dper na rgyas pa'i skye mched kyi snyoms par 'jug pa la rnam par spyod pa'i dge slong ni gcig pu gnyis su med par khang bu'am/
289b6(phal chen): sa 'am/ 'dug pa'i gnas na 'dugags// 'greng yang rung ste/ 'jig rten thams cad rgyas pa'i skye mched gang la snyoms par zhugs pa'i yul bzhin du byasam gtan pa'i yul bsam gyis
289b7(phal chen): mi khyab pas mtho 'i rnams su myong ngo // de bzhin du tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs kyis kyang yul gang la zhugs pa'i tshul bzhin du / rgyam de dag thams cad mtho ba zhing shes senyams su myong bar
290a1(phal chen): gyur to// 'di lta ste/ dper na dri za'i grong khyer rnams kyi rgyan dang lhab lhub thams cad nam mkha'i dbyings la byung ba ni yongs su snang yang / ci la'ang sgrib par mi
290a2(phal chen): 'gyur ro// 'di lta ste/ dper na gnod sbyin gyi gzhal med khang mi'i khang pa na 'dug pa'am/ mi'i khang pa gnod sbyin gyi khang pa'i khongs na 'dug pa ni phan tshun tha mi dad de/ las kyi
290a3(phal chen): yul rnam pa ji ltar dag pa'i tshul bzhin du snang ngo // 'di lta ste/ dper na rgya mtsho chen po la stong gsum gyi sdong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyang rgya'i gzugs brnyan ltar
290a4(phal chen): snang ngo // 'di lta ste/ dper na sgyu ma'i mkhan po ni sngags dang / rig sngags dang / rtsi'i mthu dang / byin gyi rlabs kyis gzugs kyi rnam pa thams cad dang / bya ba thams cad kyang yongs su
290a5(phal chen): ston to// de bzhin du tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs kyis kyang / byang chub sems dpa' byams pa'i byin gyi rlabs ye shes sgyu ma bsam gyis mi khyab pa la zhugs pas / byang chub sems
290a6(phal chen): dpa'i dbang dang byin gyi rlabs kyi ye shes chos thams cad shes pa'i sgyu ma'i stobs kyis mngon par bsgrubs pa'i mthus rgyan gyi yul rnam par sprul pa de dag mthong bar gyur to//
290a7(phal chen): de nas byang chub sems dpa' byams pas khang pa brtsegs po de'i nang du song ste/ byin gyis brlabs de dag brtul nas/ tshong dpon gyi bu nor bzangs la se gol gyi sgra byas te
290b1(phal chen): 'di skad ces smras so// rigs kyi bu 'di ni chos rnams kyi chos nyid yin gyis longs// rigs kyi bu chos thams cad ni rnam par bsgrubs na nye bar 'grub pa'i mtshan nyid de/ byang chub
290b2(phal chen): sems dpa'i ye shes kyi byin gyis brlabs pa'i rang bzhin de lta bu ste yongs su ma grub pa'o// sgyu ma dang / rmi lam dang / gzugs brnyan lta bu'o// de nas tshong dpon gyi bu ror bzangs so/
290b3(phal chen): gol gyi sgra des ting nge 'dzin de las langs par gyur pa dang / de la byang chub sems dpa' byams pas smras pa/ rigs kyi bu khyod kyis byang chub sems dpa'i byin gyis brlabs rnam par 'phrul
290b4(phal chen): ba mthong med/ khyod kyis byang chub sems dpa'i tshogs kyi mthu dang rgyu mthun pa mthong mong// khyod kyis byang chub sems dpa'i smon lam gyi ye shes kyis rnam par bsgrubs pa mthong mod/ khyod kyis byang
290b5(phal chen): chub sems dpa'i gnas mdangs dga' ba mthong mod/ khyod kyis byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa yongs su bsdu ba mthong mod/ khyod kyis byang chub sems dpa'i 'byung ba'i sgo zos mod/ khyod kyis
290b6(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi zhing gi yon tan dang rgyan tshad med pa mthong mod/ khyod kyis de bzhin gshegs pa'o smon lam rnam pa tha dad pa'i khyad par mthong mong / khyod kyis byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par thar pa
290b7(phal chen): bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i rjes su 'brang ba byas mod/ khyod kyis byang chub sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin gyi dga' ba dang bde ba myong mod// nor bzangs kyis smras pa/ 'phags pa dge ba'i bshes
291a1(phal chen): gnyen gyi byin gyis brlabs pa dang / dge ba'i bshes gnyen gyis dgongs pa dang / dge ba'i bshes gnyen gyi mthus mthong ngo // 'phags pa rnam par thar pa/
291a2(phal chen): 'di'i ming ci zhes bgyi/ smras pa/ rigs kyi bu rnam par thar pa 'di ni dus gsum gyi dmigs pa thams cad la shes pa rab tu zhugs pa'i dran pa nyams pa med pas brgyan pa'i snying po zhes bya ba ste/
291a3(phal chen): rigs kyi bu rnam par thar pa 'di lta bu brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa dag ni tshe gcig gis thogs pa'i byang chub sems dpas thob bo// nor bzangs kyis smras pa/ 'phags pa
291a4(phal chen): rgyun de dag gang du mchis/ smras pa/ gang nas 'ongs pa zer ro// nor bzangs kyis smras pa/ gang nas mchis/ smras pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i ye shes kyis byin
291a5(phal chen): gyi rlabs mngon par bsgrubs pa las 'ongs so// de ni byin gyi rlabs de nyid la gnas shing gang du'ang song ba med la 'phos pa med do// phung por gyur pa med do// tshogs su gyur
291a6(phal chen): pa med do// brtsegs par gnas pa med do// dngos por gnas pa med do// yul na gnas pa ma yin no// phyogs na gnas pa ma yin no// rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste/ dper na
291a7(phal chen): klu rnams kyi sprin gyi dra ba ni lus la'ang mi gnas/ sems la'ang mi gnas/ nang na'ang mi gnas mod kyi klu'i sems kyi dbang dang / klu'i dbang bsam gyis mi khyab par char
291b1(phal chen): rgyun tshad med pa bkye ba ni med pa ma yin te snang ngo // rigs kyi bu de bzhin du rgyun de dag kyang nang nA gnas pa'ang ma yin/ phyi rol na gnas pa'ang ma yin te/ byang chub sems dpa'i
291b2(phal chen): byir gyi rlabs kyi dbang dang / khyod kyi snong bzang ba'i phyir mi snang ba'ang ma yin no// rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste/ dper na sgyu ma'i mkhan pos ni yul thams cad yongs su bstan
291b3(phal chen): kyang 'ongs pa med/ bshig kyang gang du'ang 'gro ba med de/ 'pho ba med mod kyi/ sngags dang rtsi'i mthus yongs su mi snang ba ma yin no// rigs kyi bu de bzhin du rgyan de
291b4(phal chen): dag kyang gang du'ang song ba med/ gang nas kyang 'ongs pa med la/ gang du'ang phung por gyur pa med mod kyi byang chub sems dpa'i ye shes sgyu ma bsam gyis mi khyab pa la

291b7(phal chen): dang rten med par 'gro'o// shi 'pho dang skye ba med par 'gro'o// gnas pa dang 'pho ba med par 'gro'o// g.yo ba dang ldang ba med par 'gro'o// ltos pa dang gnas med par mo'o//
292a1(phal chen): bya/ las dang rnam par smin pa med par 'gro'o// mi skye ba dang mi 'gag par 'gro'o// rtag pa med pa dang chad pa med par 'gro'o// gzhan/

292a3(phal chen): sems can yongs su skyob pas byams pa'o// byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi 'gro ba ni gang du dga' bar skye bas tshul khrims so// byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi 'gro

292b1(phal chen): rigs kyi bu nga ni tshe'i sa yul 'phreng ba stobs kyi grong rdal khang khyim can zhes bya ba de na/ tshong dpon sa skyong zhes bya ba zhig yod de/ de sangs rgyas kyi chos la bzhag nas tshe'i sa'i mi

292b4(phal chen): tshe'i sa sreg bcu gang zhe na/ 'di lnga ste/ byang chub kyi sems ni byang chub sems dpa'i rigs su skyed pas/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi tshe'i sa'o// lhag pa'i bsam pa ni/

293a1(phal chen): rnams kyi tshe'i sa'o// theg pa chen po ni thabs mkhas pa'i rigs su skyed pas/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi tshe'i sa'o// sems can yongs su smin par bya ba ni

293a6(phal chen): lhub dang rgyan to// brtson 'grus kyi pha rol tu phyin pa ni skyed pa'o// bsam gtan gyi pha rol tu phyin pa ni spyod pa rnam par dag par byed pa'o// dge ba'i bshes gnyen rnams ni bslab/

293b7(phal chen): bcas pa'i 'jig rten dang / bdud dang bcas pa dang / tshangs pa dang bcas pa dang / dge sbyong dang bram zer bcas pa'i skye dgu'i nang na rigs la smos pa'i skyon thams
294a1(phal chen): cad kyi kha na ma tho ba med pa yin te/ sangs rgyas kyi rigs dam par skyes la/ smon lam chen po'i lus dang ldan pas rigs kyis btsun pa yin// rigs/
294a2(phal chen): kyi bu rgyud kyi rigs de lta bu dang ldan pa'i byang chub sems dpa' rnams ni chos thams cad gzugs brnyan lta bur yongs su shes pas ka 'jig rten gyi skye gnas thams cad smad pa med pa/

294a4(phal chen): bdag med par khong du chud pas// sems can thams cad yongs su smin par bya ba dang / gdul bas yongs su mi skyo'o// byams pa chen po dang snying rje chen po'i lus dang ldan pa'i phyir/

294b1(phal chen): 'khor ba'i dga' ba thams cad kyis mos par mi 'gyur ro// sgyu ma lta bu'i chos thams cad la rnam par rtse bas bdud kyi yul thams cad kyis mi gos so// chos kyi lus su byung bas/

295a1(phal chen): par spyod spyod pa'i sems can byang chub kyi sems stor bar gyur pa rnams yongs su smin par bya ba dang / 'dzam bu'i gling du skyes pa'i tshe yongs su bstan pa dang /
295a2(phal chen): lho phyogs kyi rgyud 'di'i yul 'phreng ba stobs kyi grong rdal khang khyim dang ldan pa zhes bya ba 'di'i bram ze'i rigs su skyes pa rnams dang / pha ma dang gnyen bshes su 'ong ba rnams rnam par

302a5(phal chen): chub sems dpa'i spyod yul rlabs po che la shin tu nges pa'i stobs dang shugs ni rab tu thob/ byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po mthong na thams cad mkhyen pa nyid thob pa dang 'dra bar
302a6(phal chen): ni sems/ byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po mthong bar bya ba la dbang po ni mngon du gyur/ byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po mthong bar bya ba la brtson 'grus kyi shugs chen po ni thob/
302a7(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po yongs su btsal ba la brtson 'grus phyir mi ldog pa'i sbyor ba dang ni ldan/ phyogs thams cad du mngon du gyur pa'i dbang po'i 'khor lo dang ga kun tu lta bas
302b1(phal chen): yul yongs su gnon pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i lus dang // sangs rgyas ma lus pa'i zhabs kyi drung na byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po 'jug pa'i rjes su 'brang ba'i sem/
302b2(phal chen): de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad dmigs par bya ba la yang dag par btang ba dang / byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po'i dmigs pa yongs su btsal ba dang mi 'bral ba'i bas/
302b3(phal chen): pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po mthong bar bya ba'i 'du shes kyi rnam pa'i snying po dang ldan pa'i ye shes kyi mig byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po'i lam la zhugs
302b4(phal chen): pa dang / nam mkha'i dbyings ltar yadra pa'i bsam pa dang / snying rje chen po'i rdo rje thogs po'i lhag pa'i bsam pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po'i rjes su 'brang bar smon pa
302b5(phal chen): phyi ma'i mtha'i bskal pa'i mur thug par byin gyis brlabs pa dang / yongs su gnon pa'i rtsal rnam par dag pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po'i spyod pa mnyam pa nyid kyi rjes su
302b6(phal chen): song ba dang / byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po'i sa la gnas pa'i ye shes la rnam par spyod pa// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi yul la yang dag par gnas pa dang ni ldan pa des/ byang chub
302b7(phal chen): sems dpa' kun tu bzang po de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad dang mnyam pa nyid rjes su thob pa/ dus gsum mnyam pa nyid kyi rjes su song ba/ bsam gyis mi khyad pa'i yul dang ldan pa mi
303a1(phal chen): 'phrogs pa'i spyod yul can/ mu med pa'i ye shes kyi yul dang ldan pa/ byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyis rnam par blta ba 'jig rten thams cad
303a2(phal chen): kyis zil gyis ma non pa/ 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor thams cad kyi rjes su 'brang na mngon par 'phags pa'i lus dang ldan pa de/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa rnam par snang
303a3(phal chen): mdzad kyi spyan snga na/ byang chub sems dpa'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor rgya mtshon ni 'dug/ byang chub sems dpa'i tshogs kyis ni yongs su bskor/ byang chub sems dpa'i dge 'dun ni mdun
303a4(phal chen): du byas shing / seng ge'i khri rin po che'i pad+mo chen po'i snying po can zhig la 'dug pa mthong ste/ des de'i ba spu'i bu ga thams cad las/ ba spu'i sgo re re nas kyang 'jig rten gyi khams
303a5(phal chen): thams cad kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi 'od zer gyi sprin mang po 'thon nas/ 'jig rten gyi khams chos kyi dbyings kyis klas pa/ nam mkha'i mthas gtugs pa thams cad rab tu snang bar byas/
303a6(phal chen): nas/ sems can rnams kyi sdug bsngal rab tu zhi bar byed pa mthong ngo // des de'i lus las 'od kyi dkyil 'khor sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi sprin mang po /
303a7(phal chen): dog sna tshogs can mang po 'thon te/ byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi dga' ba dang / mos pa'i shugs rgya chen po rnam par 'phel bar byed pa mthong ngo // spyi bo dang / phrag pa'i lhun gnyis dang /
303b1(phal chen): ba spu'i sgo thams cad nas kyang / spos 'od 'phro ba'i sprin gyi char kha dog sna tshogs su 'jug pa mang po mngon par 'thon nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor rgyas par/
303b2(phal chen): bkang ste/ mngon par 'bab pa mthong ngo // ba spu'i bu ga thams cad la sa ba spu'i sgo re re nas kyang / me tog thams cad kyi sprin gyi char sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed
303b3(phal chen): mang po mngon par 'thon nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor rgyas par bkang ste/ mngon par 'bab pa mthong ngo // ba spu'i bu ga thams cad las baspu'i sgo re re
303b4(phal chen): las kyang / spos sna tshogs kyi shing gi sprin mang po sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed mngon par 'thon nas/ chos kyi dbyings nam mkha'i dbyings kyi mtha' klas pa thams cad
303b5(phal chen): rgyas par bkang nas/ spos kyi shing gi sprin gyi rgyan gyis brgyan par byas te/ spos dang / phye ma dang / bdug pa'i mdzod zad mi shes pa'i char rab tu 'gyed cing / de bzhin gshegs pa thams
303b6(phal chen): cad kyi 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor rgyas par bkang ste/ mngon par 'bab par byed pa mthong ngo // ba spu'i sgo thams cad las ba spu'i sgo re re nas kyang gos sna tshogs kyi sprin mang po mngon par 'thon ce/
303b7(phal chen): chos kyi dbyings nam mkha' dbyings kyi mtha' klas pa thams cad kun nas yog par byas nas brgyan par mthong ngo // ba spu'i bu ga thams cad las baspu'i sgo re re nas kyang / dar sna tshogs kyi
304a1(phal chen): lda ldi'i sprin dang / 'phreng ba sna tshogs kyi sprin dang / mu tig sna tshogs kyi sprin dang / nor bu rin po che yid bzhin gyi sprin gyi char sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams/
304a2(phal chen): cad kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed mngon par 'thon nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor rgyas par bkang ste/ mngon par 'bab pa mthong ngo // ba spu'i bu ga thams

304a4(phal chen): snyed mngon par 'thon te/ chos kyi dbyings nam mkha'i mtha' klas pa thams cad rgyas par bkang nas/ rin po che'i shing las rin po che'i mdzod rnam par 'phro ba'i rgyan gyis brgyan par byas te
304a5(phal chen): de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor dag tu rin po che'i char chen po mngon par 'bab par byed pa mthong ngo // ba spu'i bu ga thams cad las baspu'i sgo re re nas kyang // gzugs

304b1(phal chen): mngon par 'thon te/ mngon par sangs rgyas pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa rnams la chos kyi 'khor lo bskor bar gsol ba debs par mthong ngo // baspu'i bug thams cad kyi baspu'i/
304b2(phal chen): sgo re re nas kyang 'dod pa'i khams thams cad du gtogs pa'i lha'i dbang po'i lus kyi sprin mang po mngon par 'thon te/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi chos kyi 'khor lo mang po yang da
304b3(phal chen): bar 'dzin par mthong ngo // baspu'i bug thams cad kyi baspu'i sgo re re nas kyang / sems kyi skad cig re re la sangs rgyas kyi zhing gi sprin dus gsum du gtogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams
304b4(phal chen): cad dang 'dra ba/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed mngon par 'thon nas/ chos kyi dbyings nam mkha'i mtha' klas pa thams cad rgyas par bkang ste/ sems can gnas
304b5(phal chen): med pa dang / skyabs med pa dang / rten med pa rnams kyi gnas dang / skyabs dang / rten du gyur pa mthong ngo // ba spu'i bu ga thams cad kyi ba spu'i sgo re re nas kyang / sems kyi skad cig re
